<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item
1.01. Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><i>&#160;</i></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><i>Amendment
No. 1 to the Master Loan Agreement</i></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">On
January 30, 2026, Nakamoto Inc., a Delaware corporation, through its wholly owned subsidiary, Nakamoto Holdings, Inc. (&#8220;<b>Nakamoto
Holdings</b>&#8221;), entered into that certain First Amendment to the Master Loan Agreement (the &#8220;<b>MLA Amendment</b>&#8221;<b>)</b>,
which amends that certain Master Loan Agreement, dated as of December 3, 2025 (the &#8220;<b>Master Loan Agreement</b>&#8221;), by and
between Nakamoto Holdings and Payward Interactive, Inc. (the &#8220;<b>Lender</b>&#8221;).</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The
MLA Amendment amends the Master Loan Agreement to permit the funding of a designated trading wallet maintained at the Lender (the &#8220;<b>Trading
Wallet</b>&#8221;) and to clarify that the Trading Wallet shall serve as collateral for both the obligations under the Master Loan Agreement
and obligations (if any) resulting from trading activity conducted through such wallet.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The
foregoing description of the MLA Amendment does not purport to be complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the full
text of the MLA Amendment, a copy of which is filed as Exhibit 10.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and incorporated herein by reference.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>&#160;</b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: right; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit
10.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: right"></P>

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B><U>FIRST
AMENDMENT TO MASTER LOAN AGREEMENT</U></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0.5in; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">THIS
FIRST AMENDMENT (this &ldquo;<B><I>Amendment</I></B>&rdquo;) is made as of January 30, 2026 and amends that certain Master Loan
Agreement dated as of December 3, 2025 (the &ldquo;<B><I>Master Loan Agreement</I></B>&rdquo;) between Payward Interactive, Inc. (&ldquo;<B><I>Lender</I></B>&rdquo;),
a Florida corporation, and Nakamoto Holdings Inc. (&ldquo;<B><I>Borrower</I></B>&rdquo;), a corporation organized and existing under
the laws of Delaware, with its principal place of business at 5097 South 900 East, Suite 100, Salt Lake City, UT 84117. Lender and Borrower
are each individually a &ldquo;<B><I>Party</I></B>&rdquo; and, collectively, the &ldquo;<B><I>Parties</I></B>&rdquo; hereunder.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B><U>RECITALS</U></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-right: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0.5in; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">A.
The Lender and the Borrower are parties to the Master Loan Agreement. Capitalized terms used herein without definition have the meanings
assigned to them in the Master Loan Agreement.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0.5in; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">B.
The parties hereto desire to amend the Master Loan Agreement on the terms and conditions as hereinafter set forth.</FONT></P>

as follows:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Except
as specifically amended hereby, the Master Loan Agreement shall remain unmodified and in full force and effect and the Master Loan Agreement
and each of the other Loan Documents are hereby ratified and affirmed in all respects, and the indebtedness and other Obligations of
Borrower to Lender evidenced thereby are hereby reaffirmed in all respects.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

effect to this Amendment, as follows:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

respects on and as of the date of this Amendment as though made at and as of such date (except to the extent that such representations
and warranties expressly relate to an earlier date).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0.5in; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

subject to bankruptcy, insolvency, reorganization, moratorium and similar laws affecting the rights and remedies of creditors generally
or the application of principles of equity, whether in any action at law or proceeding in equity, and subject to the availability of
the remedy of specific performance or of any other equitable remedy or relief to enforce any right thereunder. No consent, approval,
authorization or order of, or filing, registration or qualification with, any court or governmental authority or third party is required
in connection with the execution, delivery or performance by Borrower of this Amendment.</FONT></P>
